  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_5e56d9b6-dbd6-42af-9496-b76a896e4670'
      });

She’s unlike any woman he’s ever met. <br />Getting close to the girl is purely for her own protection…right?<br /><br />Lily never imagined she’d make her first real friends in captivity. <br />What lengths would she go through to keep them?<br /><br />**This is a stand alone novel and is unrelated to Friend-Zoned**</span>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/645524043?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer645524043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11537091978420476266"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382056954i/5630792._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381497240ra/4945619.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>SQUEEEE!!!!! I <u>loved</u> this book!!! 5 stars!! </b><br/><br/><i>Willing Captive </i>was the perfect blend of sexy, sweet, hilarious and deeply emotional. Both heartbreaking and heartwarming, it made me laugh, cry, and swoon!! It’s a standalone romance with a gorgeous, broody, protective Alpha hero, a sarcastic, no-nonsense, awesome heroine and a fun, action-packed, romantic plot. I highly recommend it for everyone!!<br/><br/>The first thing you should know is that this is <u>not</u> a dark romance. Trust me. I promise. Swear. Cross my </span>
  <span id="freeText11537091978420476266" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382056954i/5630792._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381497240ra/4945619.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>SQUEEEE!!!!! I <u>loved</u> this book!!! 5 stars!! </b><br><br><i>Willing Captive </i>was the perfect blend of sexy, sweet, hilarious and deeply emotional. Both heartbreaking and heartwarming, it made me laugh, cry, and swoon!! It’s a standalone romance with a gorgeous, broody, protective Alpha hero, a sarcastic, no-nonsense, awesome heroine and a fun, action-packed, romantic plot. I highly recommend it for everyone!!<br><br>The first thing you should know is that this is <u>not</u> a dark romance. Trust me. I promise. Swear. Cross my heart. This is <u>not</u> a captivity-themed book at all. Think more  along the lines of a "witness protection" type storyline instead. The hero is a genuinely a protector ;)<br><br>The story follows Lily who, thanks to her over protective family, has grown up leading a very sheltered life. But when things go south at her dad's work, she suddenly finds herself kidnapped... for her own protection.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>The mask he wears is back and looks to be leather too… it looks very steam-punk, and if I'd seen him on the street and not in my room being all creepy and shit, I would ask him where he got it... When another identically dressed, masked man appears, only bigger and taller, I figure I'm screwed. Well, that's that. Goodbye cruel world. Be sure to fuck thyself on the way out.</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Blindfolded and whisked away from her family, Lily finds it hard to believe that this was done with her best interest at heart and it takes her a while to accept their claims.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>He leans back in his chair and states, “You haven’t been kidnapped, Delilah.”<br><br>Eyes wide, I lift my face to look into his and ask, “Who are you?”<br><br>Hottie’s lip twitches. “The person who just saved your life, baby.”<br><br>What the mother fuck?</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>But the more she learns about the people who took her, the more she realizes that they're not bad guys and the head honcho, Nox, in particular has quite the soft spot underneath his tough exterior. But still...<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>I swear this guy must've been conceived though backdoor action. There's no way being that much of an asshole is natural.</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Teeheee!!!! :D<br><br>Nox was just plain awesome!! Big, badass and broody, he was a natural protector and the despite not being thrilled about his new 'babysitting' job, soon began to warm up to the snarky, sarcastic girl he'd be assigned to protect.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"You're not going to die."</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"What makes you so sure?"</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>His lip tilts at the corner and he says, "There's a reason I'm cocky, princess."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>The story is told in alternating POVs so we got both the badass side and and the snark heroine side of everything. I will admit though that there were a few things here and there that didn't fully add up to me if I thought about them too hard but nothing that brought away from my enjoyment of the story and, as you can see from the 5 star rating, nothing that affected my rating either.<br><br>Lily's point of view had me in stitches!! I swear, at least one thing on every page either made me smile, laugh out loud, or ungracefully spray tea all over my eReader. Don't judge. You'll do it too ;)<br><br>While the first half was an awesome,<em> </em>fun, almost 'lighter' reading experience, the story was also really well balanced out by some deeply emotional developments in the second half of the story that added a lot of <em>heart</em> and was what made my rating jump from a happy 4.5 to a full 5 stars.<br><br>The overall pacing was excellent!! The romance was always there but there was no insta-love at all and the banter between Nox and Lily while they were at each other's throats was just downright awesome! And this non-rushed progression this also made it so that by the time they actually started falling for each other, it and really felt believable while keeping a smile on my face.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>My eyes flutter open. I try to turn, but it seems this bed has seat belts. Looking down, I see the seat belt is actually a muscular arm winches around my waist… I realize someone is breathing into my neck and wiggling closer to me. Deeper into my butt…</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>"Is that what I think it is?"</em>
    <br>
    <br>
    <em>My drooling brain replied, "It's early, we have a hard-on pressed against our ass, and a delicious man in our bed. I'm out." Then it disconnects. </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>LOL!!<br><br>Oh and the sexy-times?? They were scorching!!! Hot, steamy, emotional and left me fanning myself!<br><br>The last 20% of the book really just took the story to the next level!! Heartbreaking, emotional, wonderful!! It gave me shivers, I totally squeed right out loud (several times) and even shed a tear or two. I absolutely <i>loved</i> how the ending took it's time and was not at <em>all</em> rushed giving us the time to bask in the happy and soak in every moment of hard earned joy.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>"Doesn't matter where you are, baby. I'll come for you… I'll come for you."</em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br><em>Willing Captive</em> had it all -- swoon, laughs, deep emotion, and a beautiful romance!! It was a perfectly paced story that gave me everything I look for in a book. You know when you finish a book and you just <em>know</em> that it was a 5 star read?? That happened here. Total book high! I loved it :)<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <em>“His arms cinch around my waist and he buries his face into my neck. He says a muffled, “Don’t wanna let you go.”</em>
    <br>
    <em>My heart swells, I whisper back, “Then don’t.” </em>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>If you're looking for a fun, exciting, romantic read that'll bring a smile to your face, having you fanning yourself and even likely make you shed a tear or two, then pick this one up!!<br><br><b> 5 stars! </b><br><br>Here's my casting for Nox and Lily:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382056954i/5630793._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382056954i/5630794._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="11537091978420476266" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_682228353" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/682228353" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/682228353?book_show_action=true">Jul 31, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer682228353" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16583909477809204013"><b>4.5 Funny Stars!</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/1fc4585e-7448-4ea6-8c50-ab5673f38dcd_zps5149af14.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381247928i/4591499.jpg' alt=' photo 1fc4585e-7448-4ea6-8c50-ab5673f38dcd_zps5149af14.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Belle Aurora is one of those authors that knows how to make me laugh. Every book I’ve read of hers has me cracking up! I love a funny book every now and then, but there is something to be said about an author that can make you laugh, make you cry, and make you feel, all in the same book! And thats exactly what this book did for me. Her characters are splendid and her writing is fantastic. This was a really enjoyable read for me! <br/><br/>Lily is a twenty two year old woman who still l</span>
  <span id="freeText16583909477809204013" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Funny Stars!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/1fc4585e-7448-4ea6-8c50-ab5673f38dcd_zps5149af14.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381247928i/4591499.jpg" alt=" photo 1fc4585e-7448-4ea6-8c50-ab5673f38dcd_zps5149af14.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Belle Aurora is one of those authors that knows how to make me laugh. Every book I’ve read of hers has me cracking up! I love a funny book every now and then, but there is something to be said about an author that can make you laugh, make you cry, and make you feel, all in the same book! And thats exactly what this book did for me. Her characters are splendid and her writing is fantastic. This was a really enjoyable read for me! <br><br>Lily is a twenty two year old woman who still lives with her parents. Not only that, she works for her dad’s company, isn’t allowed out of the house much and her best friend is her sister. She is extremely sheltered. Her father is overprotective to the extreme, but he has his reasons, as Lily soon finds out. Most of the time, Lily is okay with that. She will just stay up in her room, read and relax. She is used to her life. <br><b>
  <blockquote>Reading is my escape. It makes my brain work, which gives me a short reprieve from my isolated life.</blockquote>
</b> Sound familiar friends? Lily’s father sits her and her sister down one night to explain some recent problems his company has been having. There have been accusations, threats. Things are about to change for her. That very night, she is ‘kidnapped’. Lily tries her best to escape, but nothing seems to work. Her kidnappers quickly explain to her that they are her protecters. Nox is running the operation, along with Rock and Boo. They were hired by her father to keep her safe while all the company drama is going on. <br><br>Lily is a quirky and hilarious main character. I just loved her attitude. Then there is Nox. Nox is all kinds of mysterious, sexy and hot. And he can be an asshole at first... Lily’s description of him is pretty spot on. <br><i>
  <blockquote>Standing face to face with a still pissed off Nox, I find myself getting pissed, too. Nox just has that effect on me. I swear this guy must’ve been conceived through back door action. There’s no way being that much of an asshole is natural.</blockquote>
</i> Lily becomes close to Rock and Boo. For the first time ever, she feels she has real friends. Things with Nox are still tense. She is understanding why she is there and why it’s needed, but they constantly but heads. Lily hasn’t been around all that many guys, but there is something about Nox. Although he infuriates her, she can’t help how attracted she is to him. <br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>You know how when a guy and girl really like each other in a book, they talk about a spark between them? With Nox there is no spark. No. He bypassed the spark. When Nox touches me, there’s nothing less than the whistling, shrieking explosions of fireworks. Big ones. The ones they save till the end of the show.</blockquote>
  </b>
</i> The last thing Nox should be doing is developing feelings for someone he is protecting. He tries to keep his distance from Lily, but he just can’t stay away. As much as she aggravates him and gives him trouble, his feelings continue to grow. She is not his type at all. She’s sweet, innocent, sheltered. But he can’t help the way he feels about her. The feelings are mutual. They are both falling for one another. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/515c260b-7c52-4db8-8eb6-f30b5db0695f_zps86aa4fe6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381247928i/4591500.jpg" alt=" photo 515c260b-7c52-4db8-8eb6-f30b5db0695f_zps86aa4fe6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>“You remember what you said this morning? About it being totally stupid to fall in love with me?" <br>At that, my eyes open. He adds quietly, "Then you should start calling me a fuckin' moron.”</blockquote>
</i><br>I loved both Lily and Nox, and I loved them even more together. It made my heart smile. They had the best back and forth banter. <br><i>
  <blockquote>He’s all like ‘C’mon pack your shit’ <br>and I’m all like ‘No, I like it here’ <br>and he’s all ‘Not safe here, Princess’ <br>and I’m all like ‘Sigh. Okay.’</blockquote>
</i><br> Nox’s job is to keep Lily safe. What happens when the threat is gone? Nox’s job is secret, he is invisible, as are Boo and Rock. A relationship seems impossible. Nox will protect Lily while she needs it, but what happens next for them?<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/342aedac-c980-4df5-9c2a-f29a0c7f0531_zps7e05ecdb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381247928i/4591501.jpg" alt=" photo 342aedac-c980-4df5-9c2a-f29a0c7f0531_zps7e05ecdb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Don’t let the cover or the title fool you, this is not a dark read. It’s light hearted, sweet, sarcastic, comical and beautiful. I would recommend this book to anyone looking for something like that, you won’t be disappointed! I laughed so much, but I also cried towards the end. The last 30% or so has some seriousness to it. I also would recommend Belle Aurora’s Friend-Zoned series- that series is just as great as this book. Overall, a fantastically funny 4.5 star read! <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“That one person everyone looks for. They search and search, and some die trying to find ‘em. And when you finally meet them, something inside of you says “Oh, there you are. I’ve been looking for you. And I didn’t even know it.” </blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%203/28ecf6bd-9d45-4d40-b9c0-50e2cd0b2c9f_zps1163dd63.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381247928i/4591502.jpg" alt=" photo 28ecf6bd-9d45-4d40-b9c0-50e2cd0b2c9f_zps1163dd63.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <blockquote>‘I promised I’d come for you.’</blockquote>
</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16583909477809204013" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_692130814" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/692130814" />
    <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole"><img alt="Duchess Nicole" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499265843p2/2204947.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/692130814?book_show_action=true">Aug 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Duchess Nicole" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Duchess Nicole" href="/user/show/2204947-duchess-nicole">Duchess Nicole</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=genre-contemp-romance">genre-contemp-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=sigh-worthy">sigh-worthy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=4-star-read">4-star-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=dirty-talk">dirty-talk</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=make-me-cry">make-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=highly-rated">highly-rated</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=stand-alone">stand-alone</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2204947-duchess-nicole?shelf=e-pcs">e-pcs</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer692130814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3401844608878412402"><br/>Boy, this was all kinds of different from what I expected. I loved Belle Aurora's Friend Zoned series. When I saw this one pop up on her book list, I immediately added...then noticed the cover and name, started to be sad because I do NOT read these dark "romance" books that seem to be all the rage lately. <u>I like some sweet, some devotion, some trust and a forever kind of love. Let me tell you, that is EXACTLY what this author delivered. Belle, I will never doubt you again! </u><br/><b>
  <blockquote>"Don't push me, lit</blockquote></b></span>
  <span id="freeText3401844608878412402" style="display:none"><br>Boy, this was all kinds of different from what I expected. I loved Belle Aurora's Friend Zoned series. When I saw this one pop up on her book list, I immediately added...then noticed the cover and name, started to be sad because I do NOT read these dark "romance" books that seem to be all the rage lately. <u>I like some sweet, some devotion, some trust and a forever kind of love. Let me tell you, that is EXACTLY what this author delivered. Belle, I will never doubt you again! </u><br><b>
  <blockquote>"Don't push me, little girl. You don't wanna see my bad side."<br>I blink a second before my eyes widen and I lean back from him as I whisper hiss, "This is your good side?"</blockquote>
</b><br>This one started out really goofy/funny, as well...this seems to be the style for the author, and I love it. I love how this heroine doesn't take herself too seriously...she's just a girl, living her life, however messed up it is. So when she's kidnapped from her home one night and taken to a secret lair (house), she doesn't play the damsel in distress. Nope, she defies the sexy as hell Nox-the-captor any time she can. <br><b>
  <blockquote>"Let's face it, Nox doesn't seem like a giver of fucks."</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380900780i/3146080.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> Even when she figures out that her capture isn't what it seems, she doesn't go all gooey eyed and Stockholm Syndrome over the muscle bound kinda-hottie. The romance is slow building, which I LOVE. <b>Nox and Lily build a BOND</b>, over time and circumstance. I wouldn't call it a friendship, but it's a bond nonetheless.<br><b>
  <blockquote>"That one person everyone looks for. They search and search, and some die trying to fin 'em. And when you finally meet the, something inside of you says "Oh, there you are. I've been looking for you. And I didn't even know it."</blockquote>
</b><br>There were a couple of things that kept this from being five stars for me. The initial kidnapping was unnecessary. Why did they not simply explain things? It added drama and eventually humor, but it was completely loopy. Another point...Lily is CONSTANTLY crying. Oh, my GOSH! This girl...geez. I have to admit that under her circumstances, I'd likely have cried some as well...especially toward the end. But I started eye rolling about the tears, and when I lose that empathy for a character, it's usually hard for an author to pull me back into the story.<br><br>Fortunately, that wasn't the case here, because the last 20-30% of this book was very emotional, albeit still overly dramatic. But I loved how the author didn't stop directly after the reunion scene...she kept going and gave us more romance...since the romance was a bit lacking in the first part of the book, I felt this nicely balanced out my need for hearts and flowers.<br><br>Before I start to ramble, I'm going to conclude. Nox and Lily were both such fun characters. Nox gave me the impression of a mental <b>eye roll</b> every time he had to deal with Lily. That eye roll started morphing into an <b>interested gleam</b>, which led to some sexually charged albeit micro-moments, which then led to <b>lust-darkened</b> details that were quite simply swoonalicious. <br><br>If you go into this expecting a knock you over, deeply disturbing and evocative romance with hidden meanings and heartbreaking moments, then you may not enjoy it to it's potential. I'd suggest you go into this looking for a fun and lighthearted, somewhat unbelievable but completely engaging romance. Leaving my critic at the door, I enjoyed it very much!!!<br><br>A couple of my favorite quotes...each is very different from the other, as an example of how this book had some moments on complete opposite ends of the romance spectrum. (I laughed...a LOT. But I also got teary."<br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><b>
  <blockquote>"Then he walks over to the bed and drops the towel. And there's Nox in all his naked glory. Too bad his back's to me. I'd kill to see the front of that hard body. Stepping into his cotton boxers, he pulls them up and turns around. And there I am, staring at his fabric-covered pee-pee.<br>"Like what you see?"<br><i>Oh fuck!</i><br>He just caught me looking at his junk!<br><i>Play it cool, Lil.</i><br>Shrugging nonchalantly, I ignore my burning cheeks and reply, "Not really. I though you'd be more - more - I don't know. More impressive."<br>The ass smiles. A huge-ass smile from a huge ass"</blockquote>
</b><br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br><b>
  <blockquote>"The only way past grief is to grieve. It's the high price you pay for a love so sweet."</blockquote>
</b><br>(Now THAT is profound)<br>~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~<br>(Original post, <i>two months</i> before release date) <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[HOW does this have ratings already? Stop being petty, people...the book isn't even finished. How can you dislike it? Or like it, for that matter? It's extremely simple...don't rate until you read. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_732545777" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/732545777" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/732545777?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=addicted-to-this-author">addicted-to-this-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer732545777" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12495171868665436205"><b>5 I WANT TO BE CAPTURED BY NOX STARS.</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"I never realised how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful."</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381255922i/4602889._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='500' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Well, well, well I can honestly say I am joining the hype for this book and not holding back one bit. I loved every single word of this addictive page turner. Belle Aurora has some serious writing skills and if I thought I enjoyed her 'friend zoned' series it has nothing on this hilariously scrumptious loved up novel. From beginning to end I was glued to the pages, it felt effort</span>
  <span id="freeText12495171868665436205" style="display:none"><b>5 I WANT TO BE CAPTURED BY NOX STARS.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>"I never realised how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful."</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381255922i/4602889._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="500" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Well, well, well I can honestly say I am joining the hype for this book and not holding back one bit. I loved every single word of this addictive page turner. Belle Aurora has some serious writing skills and if I thought I enjoyed her 'friend zoned' series it has nothing on this hilariously scrumptious loved up novel. From beginning to end I was glued to the pages, it felt effortless and definitely wins out in the enjoyment awards. Forgive me if I endlessly gush, here are my 'Willing Captive' book thoughts ...<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Delilah 'Lily' Flynn lives her life in a protective bubble, her Irish born dad ensures that both his daughters are kept safe and that means that they both spend far to much time holed up in daddy's mansion. But things don't always go to plan so when the girls lives are put in danger and the family gets separated a confusing, dramatic story unfolds for the Flynn's ... Who do you trust? How will this tale end and? and what happens when Lily meets Nox, a moody over protective man who she should definitely not be falling for. 'Willing captive' is an hilarious, dramatic and romantic novel of finding love in the strangest of places<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381255922i/4602890._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>This book captures everything that I love about escaping into the written word. Bella Aurora books are confidently hilarious, heart stopping and outrageously sweet. 'Willing Captive' is the most enjoyable and entertaining book I've read all year, the one liners and dialogue are refreshingly funny and there is a honest to goodness realism to the characters dialogues that make you feel like the characters could be your next best friend. There is no unnecessary drama, just a completely refreshing storyline that has my heart squeezing and kept a smile on my face through out. The characters in this story are endlessly brilliant from the hero and heroine right up to the surrounding characters, I'm hoping to see some spin off's created in the future. Nox is the best kind of hero; moody, aloof and deliciously rugged this manly man screams of alpha male but underneath the tough exteria is a sweet and sexy man who is desperate to love and be loved, I swooned and fell in love with this protective alpha and was happy to see the author develop his character nicely throughout the story. This author hands down creates the best female heroines, I kid you not her female characters are out of the world adorable and Lily without a doubt is a smashing character. She is a bit of a ball breaker with a cute vulnerable side I never stopped laughing at her ridiculous antics and quick wit. Bella Aurora tends to have a similar formula throughout her books, comedy romance spiced up with drama and added heartfelt emotions, I loved 'Willing captive' it was a great read and I know it will certainly not be the last book I grab by this talented author.<br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>For those that appreciate a romantic comedy of sorts you do not want to miss this authors books, not only are they fantastically written but they are sweet, sexy and utterly addictive. Bella aurora is up there with my favourite authors and if you are a fan of contemporary romance I suggest that you do not miss out. Go grab it readers, enjoy ... Kisses.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12495171868665436205" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_728657422" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/728657422" />
    <a title="Catarina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina"><img alt="Catarina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514808293p2/11538033.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/728657422?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Catarina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Catarina" href="/user/show/11538033-catarina">Catarina</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11538033-catarina?shelf=cat-heart-these-books">cat-heart-these-books</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer728657422" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12144315847662401249"> <b>4,5 Captive Stars!</b><br/>	<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380792877i/3123021.jpg' width='450' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Lily is under a threat. <br/>And being the daughter of a father that is as financially healthy as he is protective, her father decides that the best for Lily is to go away, disappear until the threat goes away. <br/>So he simulates her kidnapping, except that her kidnapers are not forcefully taking her, they are transferring her to a safe house where she will stay under their protection until the danger no longer exists.<br/>And then she meets the man that is responsible for her security: N</span>
  <span id="freeText12144315847662401249" style="display:none"> <b>4,5 Captive Stars!</b><br>	<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380792877i/3123021.jpg" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lily is under a threat. <br>And being the daughter of a father that is as financially healthy as he is protective, her father decides that the best for Lily is to go away, disappear until the threat goes away. <br>So he simulates her kidnapping, except that her kidnapers are not forcefully taking her, they are transferring her to a safe house where she will stay under their protection until the danger no longer exists.<br>And then she meets the man that is responsible for her security: Nox. <br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380792877ra/3123022.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And when you’re closed in a safe house with a sexy-alpha male whose mission is to protect you… well, things heat pretty fast. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380401218ra/778438.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First things first: Main characters were both pretty damn good. And the heroine didn’t even annoyed me. (How weird is that?!)<br>Seconds things second: Supportive characters were AWESOME. I wish Rock and Boo had their own book. : (<br>And finally, what really convinced me with his book was the surprise factor. It was not predictable. Even when the plot twist happened and things got rough (It happens in all the books, don’t pretend this is a spoiler!) it still surprised me. <br>Nonetheless, it was a pretty good story, with romance and enough steam (and not dark, you may breath in relieve). <br>Go read it, now ;) </span>

<div id="review_1433418560" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1433418560" />
    <a title="Katerina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina"><img alt="Katerina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1470667070p2/5014021.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1433418560?book_show_action=true">Nov 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina" href="/user/show/5014021-katerina">Katerina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5014021-katerina?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1433418560" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8151045514990244988"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He never rushed me.<br/>He wouldn't drop me.<br/>He was my shield.<br/>He would protect me.<br/>Against almost anything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>There are two types of romances.The <b>hot-funny-lighthearted</b> ones and the <b>sucking-the-life-out-of-you</b> ones <s>yes Colleen Hoover I'm looking at you</s>.<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18071296.Willing_Captive' title='Willing Captive by Belle Aurora' rel='nofollow noopener'>Willing Captive</a> is <b>both</b>.I signed up for a fun,nothing-particularly-consuming read and instead I got an <b>action-packed,unique,strong love story</b> that clawed its way into my heart and won a place there.<br/>And <b>I loved it</b>.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422225445ra/13473986.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><b>
  <u>The story</u>
</b><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Can't h</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8151045514990244988" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He never rushed me.<br>He wouldn't drop me.<br>He was my shield.<br>He would protect me.<br>Against almost anything.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>There are two types of romances.The <b>hot-funny-lighthearted</b> ones and the <b>sucking-the-life-out-of-you</b> ones <s>yes Colleen Hoover I'm looking at you</s>.<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18071296.Willing_Captive" title="Willing Captive by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Willing Captive</a> is <b>both</b>.I signed up for a fun,nothing-particularly-consuming read and instead I got an <b>action-packed,unique,strong love story</b> that clawed its way into my heart and won a place there.<br>And <b>I loved it</b>.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1422225445ra/13473986.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <u>The story</u>
</b><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Can't help who you fall in love with, princess.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lily comes from a rich but overprotective family.As in you-dont-leave-the-house-without-an-escort overprotective.Her monotonous routine gets interrupted when she is kidnapped by people who don't fit the kidnapper profile,because they are nice and gentle to her (well except Nox).She soon finds out that they are hired by her father to protect her against anonymous death threats,and until the person responsible is discovered she has to stay under the same roof with Nox and his team.What started as the worst thing that's ever happened to her turned out to be the best,because she finally makes friends and she finds the love of her life in the handsome face of extremely annoying and gruffy Nox.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><b>
  <u>The characters</u>
</b><br>Lily was far from perfect.Self-centered,full of bullshit,she acted before thinking and never thought of the concequences.But throughout the story she became a grown-up,she fought for what she wanted and she stood by Nox,no matter what.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There are girls out there you want to fuck,and there are girls out there that you want to love.Not ashamed of you,Lily.You're not for the backround.You deserve center stage.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I can assure you that <b>alpha-male,bossy Nox</b> is every girl's dream.Yes yes he could be a huge asshole but he was also caring and protective over Lily.And man oh man his chemistry with her was off the charts.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1438248889ra/15684573.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There were also great secondary characters!I loved Boo and Rock,they were so funny and adorable!So many lol and aww scenes,they were good friends and good people despite their jobs and lifestyles.Awesome book gang alert!<br><br><b>
  <u>The feelings</u>
</b><br>The <u>first half</u> of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18071296.Willing_Captive" title="Willing Captive by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Willing Captive</a> was the <b>oh-so-smexy,panties-melting,my-brain-doesn't-function,wipe-your-mouth-you're-drooling</b> kind.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1446904078ra/16924907.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Tension,anger,fights that became seduction attempts,animal attraction and kiss-me-I'm-dying moments.Two lost souls that found a safe haven,someone to stitch their wounds,someone to turn existing into living.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You know how when a guy and girl really like each other in a book, they talk about a spark between them? With Nox there is no spark. No. He bypassed the spark. When Nox touches me, there’s nothing less than the whistling, shrieking explosions of fireworks. Big ones. The ones they save till the end of the show.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>The <u>second half</u> was the <b>rip-your-heart-from-your-chest,cry-a-<s>river</s>ocean,drown-in-despair,why-was-I-given-a-heart</b> kind.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442108376ra/16193444.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>But it was worth it.<br><br>Thank you Alexis and your perfect <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1398776402?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">review</a> that made me read this incredible story! &lt;3</span>
  <a data-text-id="8151045514990244988" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1160197355" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1160197355" />
    <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously"><img alt="Rachel Reads Ravenously" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539149211p2/14514998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1160197355?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rachel Reads Ravenously" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rachel Reads Ravenously" href="/user/show/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously">Rachel Reads Ravenously</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=ebooks">ebooks</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14514998-rachel-reads-ravenously?shelf=new-adult-mania">new-adult-mania</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1160197355" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1929035158378145637"><b> 5 stars!<br/>OMG I LOVED THIS!!!!!!!! </b><br/><br/><b> <i> “I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful.” </i> </b><br/><br/><a href='http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/willingcaptivecollage.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420777979i/13260898.png' alt=' photo willingcaptivecollage.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Literally couldn't put this one down. I cannot believe I waited so darn long to read this book! If it hadn't been for all of the awesome reviews my Goodreads friends had posted I probably never would have. That's the power of Goodreads. <br/><br/>Every once in a while you unexpectedly discover a great book, and this is one of those books. Despite the disclaimer saying this is NOT a dark r</span>
  <span id="freeText1929035158378145637" style="display:none"><b> 5 stars!<br>OMG I LOVED THIS!!!!!!!! </b><br><br><b> <i> “I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful.” </i> </b><br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/willingcaptivecollage.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1420777979i/13260898.png" alt=" photo willingcaptivecollage.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Literally couldn't put this one down. I cannot believe I waited so darn long to read this book! If it hadn't been for all of the awesome reviews my Goodreads friends had posted I probably never would have. That's the power of Goodreads. <br><br>Every once in a while you unexpectedly discover a great book, and this is one of those books. Despite the disclaimer saying this is NOT a dark read, I was very hesitant about reading this book based on the title and cover. Captive books usually aren't my thing. This book is in fact a story of finding oneself, and pretty darn funny as well. <br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Untitled.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418857558i/12924017._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Untitled.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Lily is a sheltered rich girl but her life didn't start out that way. When Lily and her sister were preteens her dad's company experienced a boom in business leaving his filthy rich. With the rise in business, so were the rise in threats to the family. More and more Lily found herself with a good book in her room than out with her friends.<br><br>One night intruders break into her family mansion and abduct Lily and her sister. I won't say much more except that not everything is as it seems.<br><br><a href="http://s177.photobucket.com/user/dawnygirl07/media/Untitled.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418857558i/12924017._SX540_.png" alt=" photo Untitled.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The mystery in this book was very well done. I always felt the undertone of suspense, even when the main characters were more relaxed in their surroundings. The author did a good job of maintaining the "what's going on?" issue because she left the reader in the dark for the most part.<br><br>I loved both Lily and Nox so much! Normally I like one main character more than the other, but Belle Aurora did such a wonderful job developing her MC's.<br><br>Lily was a great blend of cute and tough. It took her getting kidnapped to realize she wasn't living her life, that she had been spending it locked away. It became her dream to break out of her situation and live free.<br><br><b> <i> "“Books... I can’t live without books. To me, a book is better than any movie. All I need is a good book, my imagination, and I am set free. I’m in literature heaven.” </i> </b><br><br>Nox, he was a badass. He had his sweet moments but for the most part he didn't take anyone's shit. He was a bit of a jerk at the beginning of the book, but his devotion to Lily and her safety were what made him swoon worthy. I also think Nox's issues <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ near the end of the book was great. It made it more believable than him miraculously surviving. He struggled greatly to get back to Lily, a changed man, but a man still in love with her  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><b> <i> “You remember what you said this morning? About it being totally stupid to fall in love with me?" <br>At that, my eyes open. He adds quietly, "Then you should start calling me a fuckin' moron.” </i> </b><br><br>This book is humorous, suspenseful and delightful and I encourage anyone and everyone to read it.<br><br><b> <i> “Doesn’t matter where you are, baby. I’ll come for you. I’ll come for you.” </i> </b><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="1929035158378145637" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer3355099696" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1976669679951987047">5 Captive Throwdown Stars ⭐<br/><br/>Willing Captive was top notch! Where I was expecting a dark kidnapping story, it was so not. I was pleasantly surprised with the twists, the slow build romance and a sassy heroine that had me grinning foolishly. <br/><br/>Living a rich but sheltered life, Delilah (Lily) Flynn spends her days with her nose in a book. That would pretty much sum up her existence. But things get a whole lot more riveting when she is kidnapped right from her bedroom. Expecting danger, she receives pr</span>
  <span id="freeText1976669679951987047" style="display:none">5 Captive Throwdown Stars ⭐<br /><br />Willing Captive was top notch! Where I was expecting a dark kidnapping story, it was so not. I was pleasantly surprised with the twists, the slow build romance and a sassy heroine that had me grinning foolishly. <br /><br />Living a rich but sheltered life, Delilah (Lily) Flynn spends her days with her nose in a book. That would pretty much sum up her existence. But things get a whole lot more riveting when she is kidnapped right from her bedroom. Expecting danger, she receives protection of the most life changing kind…<br /><br /><b>"I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful."</b><br /><br />Nox Taylor is one of the best in his field. So you could imagine how frustrated he is at being tasked with a babysitting gig. Initially rejecting any part of this, he only agrees once the peril on Lily’s life becomes real. And once he realises how painful and beautiful this girl is, he’s pissed.<br /><br /><b>Holding up my hands in surrender, I concede, "Okay, okay. Sheesh. I’ll wear the freakin’ blindfold. Don’t get your panties in a twist, oh captain, my captain. And don’t call me Delilah."</b><br /><br />With little information Lily finds it difficult to comprehend why her life has been threatened and that her family has been split and being held separately. You watch Lily go from wallflower to spitfire while embracing and adjusting to a new life of independence and training. She also finds her interactions between herself and Nox slowly developing into more. <br /><br /><b>Biting my lip to stop myself from laughing, his eyes darken as he strides over to me, trapping me between the door and his chest. <br /><br />He mutters, "Maybe you want that. Maybe you like the idea of being a captive. Being helpless." Leaning forward, the tip of his nose brushes my earlobe and he whispers, "Does that turn you on, princess?"</b><br /><br />Perceived as the bad guy, Nox is anything but. He isn’t happy with the situation and keeping Lily safe is his priority regardless of how ruthless he needs to be. And with time, Lily is understanding that he is not the enemy and is amazing at spooning even if it is platonic.<br /><br /><b>Never had something so beautiful so close before. As soon as I walked into the bed room, I saw the changes I was dreading. <br /><br />Lily. <br /><br />She finally saw the connection. She finally felt the chemistry. And, clearly braver than I am, she finally decided to risk humiliation to find out if what we have is something worth pursuing.</b><br /><br />Gah, this book was everything I love about romance. Honestly, I can’t recommend this book enough. This book kept you guessing with an unpredictable ending you don’t see coming. We got a badass hero with a heart of gold, a genuinely likeable heroine and a side cast of characters that provided much needed light. Oh, and let me not forget the laugh out loud moments and passion that ignites. This was fabulous!</span>
  <a data-text-id="1976669679951987047" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer14789156637107448113"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/20/2014)</i></b><br/><br/><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 1/10/2017)</i></b><br/><br/><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I had this on my favorites shelf, and I am definitely going to keep it there! I took it for what it was, a funny romance with a little bit of suspense. Don't go into this expecting a suspense book first with the romance being secondary, because I don't think that's what it is - and I think that's what I enjoy so much about it! The h is awesome. She's a little quirky or even dorky, but I really enjoyed her. The onl</span>
  <span id="freeText14789156637107448113" style="display:none"><b> 5 Stars <i>(Originally Read 1/20/2014)</i></b><br /><br /><b> 4.5 Stars <i>(Re-Read 1/10/2017)</i></b><br /><br /><b>Overall Opinion: </b>I had this on my favorites shelf, and I am definitely going to keep it there! I took it for what it was, a funny romance with a little bit of suspense. Don't go into this expecting a suspense book first with the romance being secondary, because I don't think that's what it is - and I think that's what I enjoy so much about it! The h is awesome. She's a little quirky or even dorky, but I really enjoyed her. The only issue I had with the book (and the reason for my dropping it a half star) is that she cried too much. It was a really emotional time, so I get it! But I just thought it became a little too much for my liking. Other than that -- I fully enjoyed this re-read 🤗<br /><br /><b>Brief Summary of the Storyline: </b> This is Lily and Nox's story. Lily has been taken captive by Nox and his team, and she is being held in a safe house. She soon discovers that she is being held captive for her own safety and that there's is someone that wants her dead. Lily and Nox butt heads at first, but eventually they form a friendship that turns into more and they fall in love. There are some suspenseful moments, some sexy times, and some sad moments...and there is a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>POV:</b> This alternated between Lily and Nox's POV.<br /><br /><b>Overall Pace of Story: </b> Good. I never skimmed and I thought it flowed well. There are some time jumps, but I think the author handles them well and addresses the important things that happen during those times (I didn't feel like I was missing anything).<br /><br /><b>Instalove:</b> No. In the grand scheme of things...yes, things move fast. BUT I wouldn't consider this the typical "instalove" that I struggle with.<br /><br /><b>H rating:</b> 4 stars. Nox. I liked him. I appreciated how he didn't hide how he felt about the h.<br /><br /><b>h rating:</b> 4.5 stars. Lily. I loved this h! Her inner dialogue cracks me up! It felt a little dated in that I am a 35 year old woman and I understood all her humor, but I'm not sure all you youngins out there will get all the references (maybe you will 🤷🏻‍♀️). I loved that!! I just wanted her to stop crying all the time...<br /><br /><b>Sadness level: </b>Low, no tissues needed this time -- but I remember really crying the first time I read it.<br /><br /><b>Push/Pull:</b>Not really -- they both know they want each other and give in. <br /><br /><b>Heat level:</b> Good. They have some good tension, chemistry, and scenes -- but not so much it takes away from the story.<br /><br /><b>Descriptive sex:</b> Yes<br /><br /><b>OW/OM drama:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Sex scene with OW or OM:</b> No<br /><br /><b>Cheating: </b> No<br /><br /><b>Possible Triggers: </b>Yes <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Kidnapping/attempted murder/violence (on and off page), and the h was a virgin (H hadn't been with anyone in a couple years). <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>Closure: </b> I will keep this vague in hopes of not ruining it, but there is definitely a HEA ending.<br /><br /><b>Safety:</b> This one should be <u>Safe</u> for most safety gang readers<br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have cheating<br />- <b>Does Not</b> have a descriptive sex scene with OW/OM<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have the h or H pushing away<br />- <b> Does</b> have a separation between the h and H<br />- <b> Does Not</b> have abuse<br />- <b>Does </b> have a HEA ending <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer735446444" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer15230476897079541837"><b>5 Blindfold Me Anytime Stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382190300i/5743758.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"You haven't been kidnapped, Delilah." Eyes wide, I lift my face to look into his and ask, "Who are you?" Hottie's lip twitches. "The person who just saved your life, baby."</i>
</b><br/><br/><i>Willing Captive</i> was a perfect blend of <b>hilarious, romantic, heart-breaking, and swoon-worthy</b> all in one! My emotions went through the ringer with this one, for I found myself swooning one minute, then bawling the next. The characters were fantastically written and you fall in love with them al</span>
  <span id="freeText15230476897079541837" style="display:none"><b>5 Blindfold Me Anytime Stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382190300i/5743758.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You haven't been kidnapped, Delilah." Eyes wide, I lift my face to look into his and ask, "Who are you?" Hottie's lip twitches. "The person who just saved your life, baby."</i>
</b><br><br><i>Willing Captive</i> was a perfect blend of <b>hilarious, romantic, heart-breaking, and swoon-worthy</b> all in one! My emotions went through the ringer with this one, for I found myself swooning one minute, then bawling the next. The characters were fantastically written and you fall in love with them all! *cough* Rock *cough* <i>Belle Aurora</i> has just earned herself a spot on my list for now I'm hunting down everything she's ever written.<br><br><i>Willing Captive</i> was the story of a woman named <b>Lily</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382191574i/5744424.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I never realized how much I hate my life. Not until he showed me beautiful." ~Lily</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Delilah Flynn aka Lily is my kind of heroine. She's 22 years old, and has a <b>lived a life of extreme loneliness</b> due to her father's protectiveness. <br><br>Her only escape is through the hundreds of books the she occupies her time with, <b>escaping into stories and living vicariously through them. </b><br><br>She works for her fathers company but other than that spends the rest of her time at home. She's pretty much a <b>voluntary hermit</b>.<br><br>Lily's life is forever changed however, when she is <b>blindfolded and kidnapped to live a life in captivity away from her family.</b> Only problem is, she finds herself falling in love with one of her captors, Nox.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I hated the life I was living. And you changed me. All for the better. And I thank God for the day I met you." ~Lily</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Enter Lily's Captor <b>Nox</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382198698i/5748015.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Never had something so beautiful so close before."~Nox</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>While Lily is in "captivity" she has a love-hate relationship with one of her captors, Nox. Nox is the guy in charge of the operation and he is broody, cold, stoic and looks like a falling angel, not to mention he has ice blue eyes that often show no emotion. He has a job to do and Lily and her feisty attitude are not making it easy for him or his "employees". <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Been hurting a long time. You can't see this type of hurt, though. Broken hearts don't mend easily. And you're not hurting me right now, baby. But even if you were, it would hurt so sweet." ~Nox </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>As Lily and Nox are forced to spend increasing amounts of time together, an attraction begins to form which soon has both of them unable to deny their deep feelings. I'm not going to go into details about this, for it would be very easy to reveal spoilers. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382194648ra/5746261.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"This is not a sexy moment, it's a beautiful moment."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382195755ra/5746847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I read somewhere that if you're going through hell, keep going. It's the only way past it. You have to face your pain, your guilt, and your sorrow. But when the strong hands of grief capture you, it is overwhelming, and completely devastating. I fear I'll never get past the stage of hell that I'm in.."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382196664i/5747236.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Can't help who you fall in love with, Princess." ~Nox</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>When picking this one up, don't let the cover fool you. THIS IS NOT A DARK ROMANCE. It has sadness, grief, and anger but it's mostly a light-hearted romance. I would recommend this novel to everyone for it has a little something in it for everyone. Overall, this was a fantastic read!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"That one person everyone looks for. They search and search, and some die trying to find 'em. And when you finally meet them, something inside of you says, "Oh, there you are. I've been looking for you. And I didn't even know it."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1763961509" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8434567972176269992">2.5/5<br/><br/>Not as good as I expected.<br/><br/>To be honest, I don’t want to do this book review because I'm not sure what to write. Let's just say there wasn't much going on in this book and there was no earth-shattering plot here. A girl thought she was kidnapped but turned out she was protected by the professionals after her father found out that someone made multiple death threats against her, which she never knew any of these facts. Then she fell in love with her protector. Later something bad happened (bu</span>
  <span id="freeText8434567972176269992" style="display:none">2.5/5<br /><br />Not as good as I expected.<br /><br />To be honest, I don’t want to do this book review because I'm not sure what to write. Let's just say there wasn't much going on in this book and there was no earth-shattering plot here. A girl thought she was kidnapped but turned out she was protected by the professionals after her father found out that someone made multiple death threats against her, which she never knew any of these facts. Then she fell in love with her protector. Later something bad happened (but it was way too predictable), and… as you know, yeah, then… happy ending.<br /><br />The story started off well but dragged a bit in the middle. Most of interesting things happened during the last quarter of the book, but I felt like the story still kept dragging on toward the end.<br /><br /><br /><b><u>What worked for me</u> :</b><br /><br />1. The supporting characters. They were likeable and sometimes they absolutely stole the show. Perhaps they should get their own spin-off (especially Rock and Boo).<br /><br />2. The book wasn’t too long and it was easy to read.<br /><br />3. Some parts were very funny and they had me laughing out loud.<br /><br /><br /><b><u>What didn't work for me</u> :</b><br /><br />1. The plot. It was one of the most unrealistic plots I’ve ever read.<br /><br />2. Two main characters. Oh, don't get me wrong, I didn't hate them. I just couldn't connect with Nox’s character, I don't know why but I can tell it really bothered me. Lily got on my nerves at times and I found it somewhat annoying that she often acted so childish and immature though she’s 23 years old already. Honestly, I’m confused by her character. According to the story, she grew up with overprotective father, never once went out without a chaperone, had no friends, stayed home and did nothing but read her books in her bedroom most of the time, BUT she's such a badass and has a smart ass mouth. Wait! What!?? I don't get that. It was unbelievable! <br /><br />Anyway, what upset me the most about her was that she yelled and ordered her parents to get out of her room. How could she treat her own parents like this? They loved her and were there for her when she was injured and felt so miserable. I should know she’s a total spoiled brat! Gah!<br /><br /><br />Nevertheless, I didn’t hate this book but didn’t love it either. It was just way too juvenile to my taste. 3 stars is me being generous!<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8434567972176269992" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1130525289" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer1365677225430914118"><b> 2 Stars </b><br/><br/>I just dont know why, but this book had me eye rolling at everything. So this is how I arrived at my 2 Stars rating...<br/><br/><b>#1 eye roll </b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389671462ra/8047290.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The characters! Well it is understandable why I didn't really like Nox that much, because he had hardly any chapters. Most of the book was in Lilly ' s point of view and may I just to say, boy is she sooo super annoying! She got on my effing nerves. She was always so needy, it just pissed the crap out of me! Her sarcasm WASN'T SARCASM! But yeah I have got to </span>
  <span id="freeText1365677225430914118" style="display:none"><b> 2 Stars </b><br><br>I just dont know why, but this book had me eye rolling at everything. So this is how I arrived at my 2 Stars rating...<br><br><b>#1 eye roll </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389671462ra/8047290.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The characters! Well it is understandable why I didn't really like Nox that much, because he had hardly any chapters. Most of the book was in Lilly ' s point of view and may I just to say, boy is she sooo super annoying! She got on my effing nerves. She was always so needy, it just pissed the crap out of me! Her sarcasm WASN'T SARCASM! But yeah I have got to give it to her, she tried right? I didn't get her humor at all, I didnt even twitch my lips, but all the other characters seemed to get her POOR PATHETIC JOKES.. (do they even classify as jokes?). So I just went reading on and on, and when everyone was laughing, I had to go back to read the line again to look for the pun, or humor in it! And lemme just tell u how it was like...<b> LOOKING FOR DIAMONDS IN MY BATHROOM </b> yeah, it was that <b>pointless</b> . <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419313468ra/13036993.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Either she was crying or she was trying to be funny.<br> So when she got EFFING ABDUCTED, she does get scared and stuff, but her main thoughts were dominated by how her abductors looked! I MEAN JUST GIVE THIS WOMAN A NOBEL PRIZE FOR HER SMARTNESS already! Who could be this smart! I mean who cares about escape strategies when ur abductor is well built and hot right?! <br><br><br><b>#2 eye roll </b><br><br>The plot, was so monotonous. So either they were safe or they acted like they weren't safe! I mean the story moved so slowly, I thought the scientists would even discover a new planet or a civilization before this story ended!<br> So yes, I am sorry , I know I cheated on eye roll #2, this wasn't and eye roll, cuz I fell asleep right?!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419313468i/13036994.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I also didn't really get how they just fell in love! <br>So here I present to you Insta-love 101: One day they are all scowling and avoiding each other and the neXT they were just like "I, I love u like a love song baby, I , I love u like a love song baby..." (what? it's a Selena Gomez song, look it up!) There was absolutely zero chemistry. And that kids is how I met one of your great great granddads. Yup I am dead too.<br><br><b> #3 eye roll </b><br><br>The dialogues, they had no feeling! Well at least I couldn't feel a thing. To me the conversations were like they were speaking to rocks!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422773779i/13544001._SX540_.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Even these rocks have conversation skills<br> What I LOVE about Belle Aurora's writing is the beautiful lines that make me levitate! But this book had nothing. NOTHING! I didn't blush, didn't grin like an idiot and I didnt do my happy dance. I love belle aurora and this was a huge disappointment after beautiful books of hers like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17948485.Friend_Zoned__Friend_Zoned___1_" title="Friend-Zoned (Friend-Zoned, #1) by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Friend-Zoned</a><br>I thought the most interesting part of the book was finding out weather Lilly has STOCKHOLM SYNDROME OR IF SHE WAS JUST PLAIN DUMB! <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1419313468i/13036995.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>So for each eye roll I deducted a star!<br><br><br>Well on the brighter side, this book got much much better in the end! It did have those beautiful elements that make me love belle auroras books! But they weren't enough to change my whole opinion for this books. Poor baby, me!<br></span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/856287394" />
    <a title="Mona" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6013607-mona"><img alt="Mona" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565358189p2/6013607.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/856287394?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mona" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mona" href="/user/show/6013607-mona">Mona</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer856287394" class="readable"
