<span id="freeTextContainer8365934228256694820"><br/><b>**3.8 Willing to be Nox's Captive Stars**</b><br/><i>Mates, not sure I'm willing to hide my *SPOILERS*</i><br/><pre>I never realized how much I hate my life.<br/>Not until he showed me beautiful.</pre><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392630283ra/8586537.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>There was <b>laughter</b>...hysterical laughter, with some giggling on the side. And then, I experienced the tears, heartache and anxiety...all from one book. <b>Willing Captive</b> had a lot going on, for a book that started out so simple.<blockquote>
<i><b>My name is Delilah Flynn. Everyone, except my dad, calls me Lily. I spend most of my days right here, in my b</b></i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText8365934228256694820" style="display:none"><br><b>**3.8 Willing to be Nox's Captive Stars**</b><br><i>Mates, not sure I'm willing to hide my *SPOILERS*</i><br><pre>I never realized how much I hate my life.<br>Not until he showed me beautiful.</pre><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392630283ra/8586537.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There was <b>laughter</b>...hysterical laughter, with some giggling on the side. And then, I experienced the tears, heartache and anxiety...all from one book. <b>Willing Captive</b> had a lot going on, for a book that started out so simple.<blockquote>
<i><b>My name is Delilah Flynn. Everyone, except my dad, calls me Lily. I spend most of my days right here, in my bedroom.</b></i> </blockquote><b>Delilah aka Lily</b>, lives a sheltered and overprotected life. Her days are spent reading, staying in her room, or working at her fathers company. Her father takes 'protective parent' to another level. He only wishes to keep her safe...at all times. But things changes drastically...when Lily is <b>taken</b> captive. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392632944ra/8586889.gif" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>An <b>unwilling</b> captive, Lily fights, cries, rants and even attempts to <b>escape</b>...but still has no hope of returning home. She's been taken for her own protection, and must accept the circumstances she's been put in.<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>Goodbye cruel world. Be sure to fuck thyself on the way out, you mean-assed son of a whore.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote> But Lily is not so easily fooled or <b>trusting</b>. She challenges her <i>'captor'</i> at every opportunity. And tests his patience's to no end. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391687822ra/8434449.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Nox Taylor</b> isn't eager to babysit the <b>'Flynn princess'</b>. A job beneath his skills, but a job that must be done. Even if he gets the urge to be rid of the <b>sarcastic</b>, loud mouth Lily, every step of the way. <blockquote>
<i><b>You're so fucking annoying that there is nothing more I want to do than to let you go right now...but I can't.</b></i> </blockquote>Nox <b>must</b> finish the job and protect Lily at all costs. Even when pushed to the limit of his control, Nox must find the strength and patience to continue. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392636361ra/8587419.gif" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Time goes by, and weeks are spent in a safe house. Lily begins to form <b>friendships</b> with those responsible for her safety....and an un-avoidable attachment and attraction towards Nox...the hard-ass and extremely stubborn <i>hottie</i>.<blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>I swear this guy must've been conceived though backdoor action. There's no way being that much of an asshole is natural.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote>But...yes, you've guessed it, Nox <b>fights</b> the pull he feels towards Lily, by doing the only thing he can do...<b>avoid</b> her at all costs. But Lily has always held back and hidden away, so she decides to start <b>fighting</b> for what she wants...and that's, Nox. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392633693ra/8586997.gif" width="400" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'll hold back from giving more away, and just say...that's only the beginning of all the <b>shit</b> that happens and what they experiences.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392723276ra/8600642.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>Don't</b> open the spoiler, if you haven't read this book. <br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Which comes down to why my rating may be lower then most of my friends. Truth...I did love this book, but felt it was a bit over dramatized at times. <b>Too</b> much crying and overly emotional scenes from Lily, got old by the end of the book. Then the short and pretty vague perspectives we get of Nox, to me, were not enough. By the time they hook up- YES, over 60% later- I didn't really feel that I had a build up of his emotions towards her. YES more ranting... <b>What the fuck</b> happened at the end?! I can understand his gone for 6 months, comes back with an injury, but this:<br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392724169i/8600802._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Was a bit too much for me. Not that I'm against these sorts of injuries in books, I have read about other disabled characters and really enjoyed their stories. But in my opinion...not for Nox. His so macho and smug, then he comes back not sure of himself...a changed man. I just felt like it was such a fun book, then became some what serious and emotional...then it jumped to extremely sad.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <br><br><b><i>But</i>...there's always a but, even with expressing my opinion in the spoiler, I would still recommend this read. If I enjoyed it, finished it with a smile on my face...then I'll definatly recommend it to my mates xx</b><br><br><i>
  <b>"I trust you, Nox. You won't hurt me. I know it." I whisper, "I trust you."</b>
</i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391164193ra/8338456.gif" width="400" height="230" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><pre>"Don't wanna let you go."<br>"Then don't."</pre><i>**Awesome BR with my babe Pavlina**</i></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

Jeez.<br><br>At points I thought it would have been good is she just got killed and a new heroine came along that was old enough not to need a diaper and dummy anymore. I would have rated it 10 stars then! <br><br>Wait, okay so I didn't think the whole thing was shit. I enjoyed parts of it. But it would always come back to Lilly saying something just plain stupid and I'd want to throw this bloody book into a pile of shit were it belonged. <br><br>Argh it was just so frustrating. The writing, the story, Nox - none of that was awful, but when you hate the main female lead it makes it hard to enjoy. <br><br>Here are some examples - <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>"The dickhead smirks and I want to knee him in the jingle bells."</b>
</blockquote><br><blockquote>
  <b>"And there I am, staring at his fabric-covered pee-pee."</b>
</blockquote><br><br> We're suddenly all 6 years old and giggling because boys have willies<br><blockquote>
  <b>"I freeze because Nox is showering naked. And I can see his pee-pee."</b>
</blockquote> <br><br>Okay for -<br>1. Why wouldn't he be showering naked and <br>2. Again with the fucking pee-pee. Try using that in dirty talk - "Oh yeah baby let me suck that pee-pee. Errr no not your pee, ewww what are you doing. No. Stop. Oh god. Eww. Not the actual pee-pee." Sexy.<br><br>Pee-pee doesn't inspire me to think about a big hard dick, it makes me think of tiny willies weeing.<br><br>Jeez, I don't know why I bothered carrying on. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1462193225i/18964318.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

Well, okay, I will give a try and see what it's like.<br><br><b>I AM SO GLAD I DID! I LOVED IT!</b><br><br>This book had me<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/637158.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380423696ra/844299.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And more<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386525429ra/7383751.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Lily is 22 years old and leads a very sheltered life because of an overprotective father. Her life, what little she had of it, was about to change drastically when she is kidnapped.<br><br><b>
  <i>Well, that's that. Goodbye cruel world. Be sure to fuck thyself on the way out, you mean-assed son of whore.</i>
</b> ~Lily<br><br><br>Did I forget to mention that she has a potty mouth?! Lily was hilarious and I loved her throughout the whole book. </b><br><br><br>But, the more time they spend together, the more Nox is intrigued by this sexy, sassy young woman. It is his job to protect her from the threat. He can't afford to let his defenses down because if anything ever happened to her, he didn't think he could go on.<br><br><br><b>

<div id="review_733080329" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/733080329" />
    <a title="Jen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6049062-jen"><img alt="Jen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1460575899p2/6049062.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/733080329?book_show_action=true">Oct 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen" href="/user/show/6049062-jen">Jen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Jen by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4215697-steph">Steph</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=buddy-read-with-steph">buddy-read-with-steph</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=damaged-hero-heroine">damaged-hero-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=kindle-own">kindle-own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=new-adult-romance">new-adult-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6049062-jen?shelf=march-reads">march-reads</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733080329" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15489822673408563917">I am probably going to get rotten food thrown at me, as I see that most people loved this book; but for me there were a lot of things that rubbed me the wrong way! I will say that the last 70% of the story was a lot more action packed and enjoyable, and for that reason I was glad that I stuck with the book and finished. I also enjoyed Nox as a hero, and some of the secondary characters as well.<br/>My biggest issue with this story was the constant inconsistancies with Lily's character. One minute she</span>
  <span id="freeText15489822673408563917" style="display:none">I am probably going to get rotten food thrown at me, as I see that most people loved this book; but for me there were a lot of things that rubbed me the wrong way! I will say that the last 70% of the story was a lot more action packed and enjoyable, and for that reason I was glad that I stuck with the book and finished. I also enjoyed Nox as a hero, and some of the secondary characters as well.<br />My biggest issue with this story was the constant inconsistancies with Lily's character. One minute she acted like a young teenager; and then the next she was acting like her proper age of 23. I get that she had lived a sheltered life, however; when she sees Nox for the first time showering and calls his penis a "pee-pee.." I really cringed! <br />There were a few sex scenes in this book; but it was hard to get in to some of them mainly because Lily for the most part came across as so much younger. Some of the story was a little bit unbelievable to me as well.<br /><br />I don't like to be all negative though, and there were some definite positive areas in the book. The humor was hands down the highlight for me! There were some great one-liners, and even some LOL moments. I was very glad that I read to the end, and I really enjoyed the epilogue as well. One thing I can't stress hard enough, is the fact that this book is not at all a dark kidnap story. I think part of the reason for my lack of enthusiasum could have to do with the fact that I expected a totally different kind of read. I absolutely thought this would be somewhat darker than it was, even though there is a warning from the author that it isn't a dark read!<br />I did feel this was more along the lines of a YA book for the majority of the time. That is how the whole vibe felt to me..<br />So, I will sign off with these thoughts about Willing Captive. They are my opinion only, and I do know that I am the minority when it comes to this story! I didn't hate it; but it most certainly didn't "wow" me! Would I read another Belle Aurora book? Absolutely! In fact, I want to read "Raw" and am hoping that it will be a little darker than this one!!! All in all, I wouldn't steer a person away from giving this one a try; but just more warn the reader of what to expect once they crack this one open.<br /><br />Thank you to my buddies for reading this with me! Steph, BK, and Kelly♥</span>
  <a data-text-id="15489822673408563917" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=mo-money-mo-problems">mo-money-mo-problems</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=who-done-it">who-done-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=guuurrrrll">guuurrrrll</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3068938-mirjana-dtr---down-to-read?shelf=i-love-a-man-in-uniform">i-love-a-man-in-uniform</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer733740032" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1560228470717851420"><br/><b>***3 Stars***</b><br/><br/>Looks like I'm in the minority with this one. I liked it, but nothing really wowed me. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414702262ra/11679932.gif' height='281' width='500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Since there are already so many reviews out there, I'll keep this short and just list the things I did and didn't like. <br/><br/>Let's start with the positives:<br/><br/>♥ Lily's relationship with her sister, Terah<br/>♥ Lily's relationship with Boo<br/>♥ Boo and Rock - they get an extra ♥ <br/>♥ Boo anytime, anywhere. I absolutely loved her.<br/>♥ The humor - there's no denying that this book has some funny moments and definitely has </span>
  <span id="freeText1560228470717851420" style="display:none"><br><b>***3 Stars***</b><br><br>Looks like I'm in the minority with this one. I liked it, but nothing really wowed me. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1414702262ra/11679932.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Since there are already so many reviews out there, I'll keep this short and just list the things I did and didn't like. <br><br>Let's start with the positives:<br><br>♥ Lily's relationship with her sister, Terah<br>♥ Lily's relationship with Boo<br>♥ Boo and Rock - they get an extra ♥ <br>♥ Boo anytime, anywhere. I absolutely loved her.<br>♥ The humor - there's no denying that this book has some funny moments and definitely has some great lines (some I will be stealing and incorporating into my real life - Thanks Belle!)<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>I swear this guy must've been conceived through backdoor action. There's no way being that much of an asshole is natural.</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439994040ra/15915492.gif" height="281" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♥ Nox's sweet and swoony side.<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>"There are girls out there you want to fuck, and there are girls out there that you want to love. You're not for the background." Burying his nose into my hair, he mutters, "You deserve center stage."</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1431011085ra/14786670.gif" height="199" width="500" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>What I didn't like:<br><br> - Lily most of the time. Unfortunately, during most of this book she was either crying, wailing/screaming, being funny, speaking without thinking, horny, frustrating, or annoying. As you can see, the scale tips more towards the negative.<br><br> - The plot. It didn't make much sense. A head scratcher for me. Nothing feels fully explained and hashed out. You were given a half assed reason and expected to just believe it.....TA DA, here's why. That didn't work for me. Too many glossed over or omitted details that are needed to give some meat to the story.<br><br> - Nox's history and background. We don't really get much of it. What IS his job? What DOES his team do? Who IS he? How did he get into this line of work? Why bring up his nasty scar if you're not going to say how he got it? No real character development. I didn't feel like I knew him at all. <br><br> - The connection between Nox and Lily. I just didn't feel it. Too much was "told" to me, without letting me "feel" anything. I had no vested interest in the two of them as a couple. It all felt forced.<br><br> - The writing style. It just didn't gel with me. <br><br>This is my first Belle Aurora book and I'm not sure if we're a good fit. Though I'm told I really need to read Friend Zoned, so maybe it's just a matter of the book and not the author. </span>

<div id="review_737455598" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/737455598" />
    <a title="Michelle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle"><img alt="Michelle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1505605297p2/13126896.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/737455598?book_show_action=true">Oct 08, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Michelle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Michelle" href="/user/show/13126896-michelle">Michelle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer737455598" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16079744716276893366"><b>Disclaimer... <br/>Okay so I read the statement "This is NOT a dark romance about a million times. But then my brain decided to go on vacation and I seriously started thinking, okay... she must mean, this is not a HEA dark romance... then I started the book and it hit me. This is NOT a dark romance, as in not a freaking dark romance. I finally got it! Yay me! </b><br/><br/>Delilah 'Lily' Flynn hasn't been handed much freedom in her young life. With an overprotective father who doesn't let her wander too far, she h</span>
  <span id="freeText16079744716276893366" style="display:none"><b>Disclaimer... <br>Okay so I read the statement "This is NOT a dark romance about a million times. But then my brain decided to go on vacation and I seriously started thinking, okay... she must mean, this is not a HEA dark romance... then I started the book and it hit me. This is NOT a dark romance, as in not a freaking dark romance. I finally got it! Yay me! </b><br><br>Delilah 'Lily' Flynn hasn't been handed much freedom in her young life. With an overprotective father who doesn't let her wander too far, she hasn't experienced much of life. She's never been kissed, never dated, never fell in love. But all of that is about to change, because as well all know, being kidnapped makes one hell of a first impression.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388896634i/7951960.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Nox Taylor is good at what he does. Just what is that job? Protect and eliminate the threat. But Lily is unlike any job he's ever had before. He knows he has to gain her trust but he also knows he can't get to close to her. It's a difficult balance to keep, until he just has no choice in the matter - there's just something about her that has gotten under his skin.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388896634i/7951961.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lily's been separated from her family and she wants answers. Unsure if she can trust what Nox and her other captors, Boo &amp; Rock, tell her is the truth. Nox knows his job isn't an easy one, just one he happens to be good at. But if there is no trust, protecting her will be that much harder. He's got to give a little to prove that he is being honest with her. Her life is in danger, it's just that the threat isn't from the group to took her.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388896634i/7951962.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Nox was a complete Alpha, but not that type that is a bit over the top. He is confident and just the right amount of cocky. Spending too much time with Lily has him questioning his ability to do his job, but staying away is just no longer an option.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388896634i/7951963.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don't remember the last time I read a book that had me laughing to the point of tears and then crying like a baby. Lily was such a breath of fresh air, her character was all sorts of snarky and smart ass. Any small trait that normally could cause some involuntary eye rolling just did not exist. <br><br><i>
  <b>"I swear this guy must've been conceived through some backdoor action. There's no way being that much of an asshole is natural."</b>
</i> <br><br>This story had so much of a little bit of everything that just made one perfect story. There were moments where Nox was frustrating and sweet, and you craved every second of it. This was my first Belle Aurora read and it was a winner. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388896634i/7951964.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>There was such a light feel to this story because of the comical banter, but this story wasn't just all laugh out loud moments. We still had a story were Lily was in danger and that all had to be sorted out, that is when the emotional trip to hell begins. I held on, until I couldn't hold on any longer. Once I gave into the emotions and felt all the hurt, finally trading in the laughter for embarrassing sobs, I was pulled slightly back from the ledge. That part of the story for me turned what was happily sitting around a 4 to a 5 star read. I am not sure how she got the timing perfect, but it was perfection. <br><br>This story was a great introduction to Belle Aurora's writing and I have a feeling that this will not be the last book of hers that I will be reading or rating 5 stars. <br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16079744716276893366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer2481618274421479698">4.5 Stars!<br/><br/>Love Belle Aurora and this one definitely didn't disappoint! She brought her trademark humor, a sexy alpha male, some suspense and intrigue....a few tears and some hot sexy times! <br/><br/>So....this was a lot different then what I was expecting. You look at the cover and you read the blurb, you see kidnapping and you think possibly dark and twisted! Yeah....nope! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/630174.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was more of a romantic comedy with a splash of suspense. And it was perfect. I laughed, I cried, I swooned. Nox....oh my! Nox w</span>
  <span id="freeText2481618274421479698" style="display:none">4.5 Stars!<br><br>Love Belle Aurora and this one definitely didn't disappoint! She brought her trademark humor, a sexy alpha male, some suspense and intrigue....a few tears and some hot sexy times! <br><br>So....this was a lot different then what I was expecting. You look at the cover and you read the blurb, you see kidnapping and you think possibly dark and twisted! Yeah....nope! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/630174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was more of a romantic comedy with a splash of suspense. And it was perfect. I laughed, I cried, I swooned. Nox....oh my! Nox was all kinds of yummy! <br><br>Lily is a 20-something still living at home with her over-protective parents. She wasn't allowed to go to college, she doesn't date, she works for her dad, she reads. But she's spunky, and fun, and quirky and strong and I loved her. <br><br>I don't want to say too much without giving too much of the story away. Bottomline, Lily is "kidnapped"...but it's more for protection then anything else. While being protected she starts to discover what it's like to have friends and relationships with other people, something she's never experienced before. Lily grows close with Nox, who is in charge of protecting her. <br><br>I thought Nox and Lily's relationship developed at the perfect pace. It wasn't insta-love or anything like that. There was great sexual tension and chemistry between them. And I liked seeing Lily kind of come out of her shell and explore and experience things. <br><br>The banter between all of the characters had me laughing out loud. The threat still lingers, and through all of the humor there were some really intense and exciting moments. The last 20% of the book was really intense. I was scared, I cried, I screamed.....I was all over the place emotionally. And I loved the way everything came together at the end.<br><br>I <b>LOVE</b> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6983012.Belle_Aurora" title="Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Belle Aurora</a>....and if you haven't read her other series <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17948485.Friend_zoned__Friend_Zoned___1_" title="Friend-zoned (Friend-Zoned, #1) by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Friend-Zoned</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17730406.Love_Thy_Neighbour__Friend_Zoned___2_" title="Love Thy Neighbour (Friend-Zoned, #2) by Belle Aurora" rel="nofollow noopener">Love Thy Neighbour</a>...what are you waiting for??? Who doesn't love books with hot alpha men that make you laugh?!?!?! <br> </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer10048686875878542160"><strong>****4 Romantic Comedy Stars****</strong><br/><br/>I picked this book because of a status update from one of my BBF's on Goodreads - I just saw the word "pee-pee" and couldn't believe how an author could fit that word into a book about kidnapping.<br/><br/>Well, I wasn't disappointed - I was cracking up throughout the book with how naïve and cute Lily was.  She was a feisty little thang!<br/><br/>Lily comes from a very rich family and her life is in danger.  Someone is sending threatening letters to her father's company.  This is wher</span>
  <span id="freeText10048686875878542160" style="display:none"><strong>****4 Romantic Comedy Stars****</strong><br><br>I picked this book because of a status update from one of my BBF's on Goodreads - I just saw the word "pee-pee" and couldn't believe how an author could fit that word into a book about kidnapping.<br><br>Well, I wasn't disappointed - I was cracking up throughout the book with how naïve and cute Lily was.  She was a feisty little thang!<br><br>Lily comes from a very rich family and her life is in danger.  Someone is sending threatening letters to her father's company.  This is where Nox and his crew come in to kidnap Lily from her home and keep her safe. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380976576i/3635434.png" alt="" width="274" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nox is ALPHA!! Way, way Alpha and they continue to butt heads which brings in the comedy....but not only is it funny....Belle Aurora incorporates so many other emotions throughout the book.  Even to the point where I teared up.</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer744649305" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1927476243667390281"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg' width='125' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'Funny Kidnapped' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br/><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431505ra/865936.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I wasn't expecting what I got when I started this book. I knew it wasn't a dark read. But what I got was just so freaking awesome! I laughed my pants off. I LOVED it all!! And I loved the characters!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"Can't help who you fall in love with, Princess."<br/><br/>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg' width='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383588348i/6602716._SX540_.jpg' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br/><br/>"Not ashamed of you, Lily."<br/><br/>He stops speak</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText1927476243667390281" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380408658i/799615._SX540_.jpg" width="125" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>♥♥♥ 4.5 'Funny Kidnapped' Stars ♥♥♥</b><br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380431505ra/865936.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I wasn't expecting what I got when I started this book. I knew it wasn't a dark read. But what I got was just so freaking awesome! I laughed my pants off. I LOVED it all!! And I loved the characters!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Can't help who you fall in love with, Princess."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383588348i/6602716._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Not ashamed of you, Lily."<br><br>He stops speaking for a moment, allowing that to sink in.<br><br>"You're not for the background." Burying his nose into my hair, he mutters, "You deserve center stage."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Delilah 'Lily' Flynn is a twenty-two years old woman, who lives with her parents and sister. Her parents, especially her father, have kept her very overprotected from her surroundings and people for fear that something bad will happen to her, due to their wealth. Because of that, Lily works for her father where she can be watched carefully. In order for her life not to be dull, she has found her heaven in reading books and living vicariously through them. She absolutely LOVES reading, and I can totally relate. Nothing much ever happens in her life, until one day that changes. There have been some threats made and in a blink of an eye, she finds herself carted off blindfolded. She has been 'kidnapped' by Nox Taylor.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I trust you, Nox. You won't hurt me. I know it." I whisper, "I trust you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Lily was such a freaking hoot! I LOVED her! Her hilarious inner ramblings had me chuckling a lot. She was just herself and didn't pretend to be anyone else, which I loved. She had a fiesty temper and was fully of witty, snarky comments. Seriously, it was hard not to like her. I have never laughed so much from someone getting 'kidnapped'. Which, she later finds out was not the case. She was being rescued by Nox, Rock, and Boo. Three badass characters who I loved so much, as well. There were a few parts that dragged on a little bit, but for the most part, this book was really entertaining. I couldn't wait for Lily and Nox to start having their arguments. They disliked each other in the beginning, but underneath that dislike there was very much a like in there as well. As time went on, having to spend their days in close quarters, their attraction grew until they had find out if what they felt was real.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383589287i/6603046._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"He's like a fairy-tale hero for Christ's sake... He's all like 'C'mon, pack your shit' and I'm all like 'No, I like it here' and he's all 'Not safe here, princess' and I'm all like 'Sigh. Okay.'<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Oh Nox... When I started this book, Nox kinda freaked me out a bit. He was mean in the way he protected her. But that's because he took her safety seriously. He didn't like playing games and was clear in what he expected of her. But Lily, was rebellious. The interactions between these two characters had me laughing, swooning, and melting. I really thought Nox was a jerk, but soon my view of him changed. With the months passing by, he came to feel for Lily. More than just a hired protector taking care of his protectee. He is drawn to her strong personality and actually loves that about her, despite their arguments. I loved seeing them slowly let their guard down.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"I don't feel lonely when I'm with you."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>In the second half of the book, I completely LOVED Nox. He was just so freaking swoony at times. He made my heart and panties melt. I freaking LOVED his dirty alpha mouth. It. Was. The. Best. He also had a sweet sensitive side that I loved just as much. And then he had such awesome team members, Rock and Boo. These two were so great and became amazing friends to Lily, which she hasn't had in a really long time. Rock and Boo were a badass couple. I was so glad that Nox had a guy friend in Rock to talk to. And Lily had Boo. Boo was such an awesome chick or like Rock says about her 'Badass with a hint of lady.' I loved her. They were really supportive of Nox and Lily when it became obvious that they had feelings for one another. Any moment with Nox and Lily, thereafter, made me sigh. I loved them both separately and together they were even better. They brought out all the good in each other. <br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383592678ra/6604145.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●<br><br>"Don't wanna let you go."<br><br>My heart swells. I whisper back,"Then don't."<br><br>●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●  ●</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>This book was really awesome. It had some sexy steamy moments, funny laugh out loud moments, and even sad moments. All of it was good. I loved every single character in this book. Like I said, the only thing was that there were a few times where it felt like it dragged on a little bit. It was still very good, though. The ending had me tearing up, even though I had a feeling that is what would end up happening. I still enjoyed it. It was really sweet romantic comedy. I thoroughly enjoyed this and would recommend you to give this a read. It was just really good. And I'm kind of hoping Rock and Boo will get their own book, cuz I loved them to pieces as well. We'll see if that happens. *fingers crossed*<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794785i/596848._SX540_.jpg" width="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="1927476243667390281" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_727649277" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/727649277" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/727649277?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=4-star-books">4-star-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer727649277" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3622694815750903220"><a href='http://imgur.com/4pkNxiO' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381839830i/5342725._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>Author Interview + More - > <a href='http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/giveaway-author-interview-willing.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>HERE</a></b><br/><br/><b>4 Captivating Stars</b><br/><br/>I didn’t read the disclaimer to this book, so just to let everyone know, this isn’t a dark book. Now, that’s out of the way, I want to say Willing Captive is a light-hearted read and my first Belle Aurora book.<br/><br/>Lily is taken from her home. She’s confused and scared. Nox is the one in charge of her and baby-sits Lily. Lily is a stubborn, head-strong girl and makes it hard for Nox to keep her in check. All of this goes on, while Lily’s life is </span>
  <span id="freeText3622694815750903220" style="display:none"><a href="http://imgur.com/4pkNxiO" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381839830i/5342725._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Author Interview + More - &gt; <a href="http://www.jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/2013/10/giveaway-author-interview-willing.html" rel="nofollow noopener">HERE</a></b><br><br><b>4 Captivating Stars</b><br><br>I didn’t read the disclaimer to this book, so just to let everyone know, this isn’t a dark book. Now, that’s out of the way, I want to say Willing Captive is a light-hearted read and my first Belle Aurora book.<br><br>Lily is taken from her home. She’s confused and scared. Nox is the one in charge of her and baby-sits Lily. Lily is a stubborn, head-strong girl and makes it hard for Nox to keep her in check. All of this goes on, while Lily’s life is threaten.<br><br>First off, there’s not a lot of pre-BS in this book. What do you mean? Lily is taken in chapter one. I like this. Sometimes when I read kidnapping books and there’s a lot of pre-character development I get a little side-track and bored. It’s a pretty fast pace book that keeps you on your toes.<br><br>Lily is a strong girl and I’m starting to like these girls. She doesn’t go down without a fight. And Nox, oh man, I like him. He’s a big burly guy and it’s kind of adorable how he interacts with Lily. Oh they have major banter and there’s plenty of push back on both parts.<br><br><a href="http://imgur.com/U0ILwPK" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1381839830i/5342726._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>That one person everyone looks for. They search and search, and some die trying to find ‘em. And when you finally meet them, something inside of you says 'Oh, there you are. I’ve been looking for you. And I didn’t even know it.'</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I even like the side characters, the people who also guard Lily. I laughed at many of the parts and overall the story was interesting. The read isn’t overly steamy, but there are steamy parts. Lily did frustrate me at times. I think it was her “innocence” I kind of had a problem with. Shocking I know. I usually am all for the sweet girl, but maybe I couldn’t mix a strong and sweet girl at the same time.<br><br>Not the entire story is about Lily being held as a captive and I liked that. The book shifts towards the end and it adds so much bam to the story. I was kind of shocked by the change of direction, but that doesn’t mean I didn’t gobble it up.<br><br>It’s a light-hearted book with a kind of kidnapping theme and if that is your thing, then Willing Captive is for you. I’m a fan of Belle Aurora and I can’t wait for my next book by her.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3622694815750903220" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked

    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer6862711044309761397">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br/>At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home. She stumbled across Sandra Brown’s Breath of Scandal and fell in love with romance.<br/>Having been brought up in a loud and boisterous family of Croatian descent, she developed a natural love for dramatics and laughte</span>
  <span id="freeText6862711044309761397" style="display:none">Belle Aurora is thirty-something year old and was born in the land down under. <br />At an early age she fell in love with reading. Boredom one summer had her scouring the bookshelves at home. She stumbled across Sandra Brown’s Breath of Scandal and fell in love with romance.<br />Having been brought up in a loud and boisterous family of Croatian descent, she developed a natural love for dramatics and laughter. Only some years ago had she discovered a new love. <br />Humorous romance novels.<br />So many authors had opened a brand new world where she could lose herself yet feel safe and at home in their stories. Belle has been known to become a screeching banshee while anxiously awaiting their newest titles.<br />Belle never thought she would write. It had never interested her until recently. Friend-Zoned began to form and in February this year Belle typed the words Chapter One. And she fell in love.<br />With words.<br />With writing.<br />With a creative imagination she never knew she harbored.<br /><br />Belle Aurora is a USA Today best-selling author.</span>
